          throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object');

              // Avoid bugs when hasOwnProperty is shadowed
              if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(nextSource, nextKey)) {
                to[nextKey] = nextSource[nextKey];
              }
            }
          }
        }

      },
      writable: true,
      configurable: true
    });

      return;

  <script>
   // delay Google ads loading on mobile and ipad (for better performance): load it after user scrolls 50% of the screen height
      (function(){
        // Don't load ads on US mobile devices
        var country = '';
        if ( 'US' === country ) {
          var mq = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 601px)');
          if ( mq.matches ) {
            console.log('Google Ads not loaded.');
            return;
          }
        }

        function throttle (fn, wait) {
          var time = Date.now();
          return function() {
            if (throttleWaitTimePassed(time, wait)) {
              fn();
              time = Date.now();
            }
          }
        }
        function throttleWaitTimePassed (time, wait) {
          return (time + wait - Date.now()) < 0;
        }
        const halfOfTheScreen = document.documentElement.clientHeight / 2;
        function loadAds () {
          if (window.pageYOffset < halfOfTheScreen) {
            return;
          }
          importGptScript();
          window.removeEventListener('scroll', throttleLoadAds);
        }
        function importGptScript () {
          const tag = document.createElement("script");
          tag.async=true;
          tag.className="gptads";
          tag.src="https://securepubads.g.doubleclick.net/tag/js/gpt.js";
          const node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
          node.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, node);    
        }
        function getCookie(name) {
          const value = "; " + document.cookie;
          const parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
          if (parts.length == 2) return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
        }

        const throttleWait = 200;
        const desktopMinSize = 960;
        const throttleLoadAds = throttle(loadAds, throttleWait);
        if (getCookie('banner-ad-hide')) {
          return;
        } else if (document.documentElement.clientWidth > desktopMinSize) {
          importGptScript();
        } else {
          window.addEventListener('scroll', throttleLoadAds);
        }
      })();
  </script>

       <h2 class="contentStrip__title">
        How can Finder help?
       </h2>
       <div class="contentStrip__summary">
        <p>
         The Finder team is dedicated to making your life decisions a whole lot easier. As Australia's largest comparison site with 2 million visitors each month (Nielsen), we compare virtually everything. Were 100% free and privately owned (not by a bank or an insurance company). We're on your side!
        </p>

    <h3>
     Important information about this website
    </h3>
   </div>
   <div class="modal-body">
    <p>
     finder.com.au is one of Australia's leading comparison websites. We compare from a wide set of banks, insurers and product issuers. We value our editorial independence and follow
     <a href="https://www.finder.com.au/editorial-guidelines" rel="nofollow">
      editorial guidelines
     </a>
     .
    </p>
    <p>
     finder.com.au has access to track details from the product issuers listed on our sites. Although we provide information on the products offered by a wide range of issuers, we don't cover every available product or service.
    </p>
    <p>
     Please note that the information published on our site should not be construed as personal advice and does not consider your personal needs and circumstances. While our site will provide you with factual information and general advice to help you make better decisions, it isn't a substitute for professional advice. You should consider whether the products or services featured on our site are appropriate for your needs. If you're unsure about anything, seek professional advice before you apply for any product or commit to any plan.
    </p>
    <p>
     Products marked as 'Promoted' or 'Advertisement' are prominently displayed either as a result of a commercial advertising arrangement or to highlight a particular product, provider or feature. Finder may receive remuneration from the Provider if you click on the related link, purchase or enquire about the product. Finder's decision to show a 'promoted' product is neither a recommendation that the product is appropriate for you nor an indication that the product is the best in its category. We encourage you to use the tools and information we provide to compare your options.
    </p>
    <p>
     Where our site links to particular products or displays 'Go to site' buttons, we may receive a commission, referral fee or payment when you click on those buttons or apply for a product. You can learn more about how we make money
     <a href="https://www.finder.com.au/how-we-make-money" rel="nofollow">
      here
     </a>
     .
    </p>
    <p>
     When products are grouped in a table or list, the order in which they are initially sorted may be influenced by a range of factors including price, fees and discounts; commercial partnerships; product features; and brand popularity. We provide tools so you can sort and filter these lists to highlight features that matter to you.
    </p>
    <p>
     We try to take an open and transparent approach and provide a broad-based comparison service. However, you should be aware that while we are an independently owned service, our comparison service does not include all providers or all products available in the market.
    </p>
    <p>
     Some product issuers may provide products or offer services through multiple brands, associated companies or different labelling arrangements. This can make it difficult for consumers to compare alternatives or identify the companies behind the products. However, we aim to provide information to enable consumers to understand these issues.
    </p>
    <p>
     Providing or obtaining an estimated insurance quote through us does not guarantee you can get the insurance. Acceptance by insurance companies is based on things like occupation, health and lifestyle. By providing you with the ability to apply for a credit card or loan, we are not guaranteeing that your application will be approved. Your application for credit products is subject to the Provider's terms and conditions as well as their application and lending criteria.
    </p>
    <p>
     Please read our website
     <a href="https://www.finder.com.au/terms-and-conditions" rel="nofollow">
      terms of use
     </a>
     and
     <a href="https://www.finder.com.au/privacy-policy" rel="nofollow">
      privacy policy
     </a>
     for more information about our services and our approach to privacy.
    </p>

  <script>
   // TVC Modal
  var modal = document.querySelector(".js-tvc-modal");
  var openModal = document.querySelector(".js-tvc-open-modal");
  var closeModal = document.querySelector(".js-tvc-close-modal");
  var modalOverlay = document.querySelector(".js-tvc-modal");
  var modalHeader = document.querySelector(".luna-modal__header");
  var modalBody = document.querySelector(".luna-modal__body");
  var frame = document.getElementById("tvc");

  var close = function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    modal.classList.remove("is-visible");
    modal.setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    openModal.focus();
    frame.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"pauseVideo","args":""}', '*');
  };

  if (modal) {
    // Shows the modal
    openModal.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      modal.classList.add("is-visible");
      modal.setAttribute("aria-hidden", "false");
      frame.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"playVideo","args":""}', '*');
    });

    // Calls the close function and closes the modal
    closeModal.addEventListener("click", close);

    // Stops the event bubbling from the chain
    modalHeader.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    // Stops the event bubbling from the chain
    modalBody.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
    });

    // Modal closes when the overloay is clicked
    modalOverlay.addEventListener("click", close);

    // Will cycle focus within the modal when the tab key is pressed
    closeModal.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
      if (e.keyCode == 9) {
        e.preventDefault();
        modal.focus();
      }
    });

    // Shift + Tab keys at top of modal cycle focus back to last focusable element at bottom of modal
    modal.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
      if (e.shiftKey && e.keyCode == 9) {
        e.preventDefault();
        closeModal.focus();
      }
    });

    // Modal will close when the escape button is pressed
    document.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
      if (e.keyCode == 27) {
        close(e);
      }
    });
  }
  </script>

  <script id="optimizely-params-js-before" type="text/javascript">
   function updateSessionParameters() {
    function URLSearchParamsPolyfill(searchString) {
        var self = this;
        self.searchString = searchString;
        self.get = function (name) {
            var results = new RegExp('[\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)').exec(self.searchString);
            if (results == null) {
                return null;
            } else {
                return decodeURI(results[1]) || 0;
            }
        };
    }
    function createUrlSearchParams (url) {
        if (window.URLSearchParams) {
           return new window.URLSearchParams(url);
        }
        // IE only
        return new URLSearchParamsPolyfill(url);
    }
    
    function addCookie(name, value) {
        const cookie = name + "=" + value + "; expires=0;path=/;";
        document.cookie = cookie;
        return cookie;
    }
    
    function updateUtmParam(urlSearchParams, key) {
        const utmParam = urlSearchParams.get(key);
        if (!utmParam) {
            return;
        }

        addCookie('optimizely_' + key, utmParam);
    }

    const urlSearchParams = createUrlSearchParams(window.location.search);
    updateUtmParam(urlSearchParams, 'utm_source');
    updateUtmParam(urlSearchParams, 'utm_medium');
}

updateSessionParameters();
const localStorageKey = 'finder/optimizely.hasBeenFinderStaff';
const storedIsFinderStaff = window.localStorage.getItem(localStorageKey) === 'true';
if (!storedIsFinderStaff && false) {
        window.localStorage.setItem(localStorageKey, false);
}
  </script>
